> 一张详细的提示，用于生成一张年轻女性（约瑟芬·兰福德）在夜晚的现代咖啡馆里，以智能手机风格拍摄的抓拍照片。照片中，她正在逗趣地撅嘴做亲吻状，同时轻柔地抚摸着膝盖上的一只橘色虎斑猫，强调温暖的环境光和焦外虚化效果。

  "prompt_elements": {

      "description": "Young woman with long, voluminous wavy blonde hair",

    },

      "top": "White ribbed fitted tank top",
      "bottoms": "Blue denim shorts with frayed hem"
    },
    "action": {
      "pose": "Sitting relaxed on a textured sofa, legs crossed",
      "interaction": "Gently petting a sleeping orange tabby cat on lap, hand scratching cat's head"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Modern cafe or lounge interior at night",
      "background": "Large glass windows, reflection of warm globe lights, 'no smoking' sign on glass, cartoon cat sticker on window",
      "furniture": "Woven wicker or textured grey sofa, dark tables"
    },
    "technical": {
      "lighting": "Warm ambient indoor lighting, bokeh background lights, soft flash or direct illumination on subject",
      "style": "Candid smartphone photography, realistic 8k, casual snapshot",
      "angle": "Eye-level or slightly high angle medium shot"
    }
  },
  "full_prompt_string": "A realistic candid photo of a young woman with long wavy blonde hair making a playful kissing face while sitting in a cafe. She is wearing an oversized blue bomber jacket, white top, and denim shorts. She is gently petting a fluffy orange tabby cat sleeping on her lap. ### 18. 伊斯坦布尔黄金时段的电影感现代都市场景

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的提示，旨在生成一张超逼真的电影剧照，描绘一对情侣在当下伊斯坦布尔的黄金时段。该提示细致地定义了场景的氛围（温暖、真实、亲密的瞬间）、互动（并肩行走，稍作停顿，没有身体接触，手持咖啡/糕点）以及技术限制（4:5 纵向构图、超高分辨率、自然动态范围、完美解剖学检查）。它要求上传男性和女性对象的参考图像。

![伊斯坦布尔黄金时段的电影感现代都市场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927702494_cb00sf_HAByzBCXMAAUk1W.jpg)

{
  "generation_request":{
    "meta_data":{
      "tool":"NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type":"cinematic_modern_city_scene_google_safe",

      "priority":"highest"
    },

      "female":"UPLOAD_REF",
      "male":"UPLOAD_REF"
    },

    "output_settings":{
      "aspect_ratio":"4:5",
      "orientation":"portrait",
      "resolution_target":"ultra_high_res",
      "render_style":"ultra_photoreal_cinematic_film_still",
      "film_grain":"subtle_fine_grain",
      "dynamic_range":"natural_not_hdr",
      "color_grade":"warm_golden_hour_soft_skin"
    },

    "anatomy_and_realism":{
      "perfect_anatomy":true,
      "accurate_hands":true,
      "accurate_eyes":true,
      "natural_body_proportions":true,
      "no_extra_fingers":true,
      "no_missing_fingers":true,
      "no_face_warp":true
    },

    "global_constraints":{
      "no_nudity":true,
      "no_suggestive_content":true,
      "no_physical_contact":true,
      "no_text":true,
      "no_logos":true
    },

    "creative_prompt":{
      "scene_summary":"Present-day {argument name="city" default="Istanbul"}, golden hour fading into early evening. A close, warm city moment that feels real.",

      "foreground_story":"They walk extremely close, almost shoulder-to-shoulder but not touching. They slow down for a second as if the city around them disappears. The woman holds a small paper cup near her chest with both hands. The man holds a small paper bag (pastry) slightly lifted as if offering it—without reaching toward her. She looks up at him with a soft, genuine smile; he leans his head slightly closer (no contact) and smiles back. Their eye contact lasts a beat longer than normal, then both look forward again and continue walking. Hands are clearly visible, relaxed, separate.",

      "background_story":"Warm street lamps begin to glow. The Bosphorus is visible at the end of the street with a distant ferry passing. A calm street cat sits on a low wall near them, quietly present. The pavement has subtle golden reflections as if it was lightly cleaned or slightly damp, adding cinematic texture without rain.",

      "environment_details":"Authentic Istanbul textures: worn stone pavement, warm window glow shapes, old facades, soft bokeh from lamps, no readable signs, no modern billboards, few people far behind out of focus so they feel alone in the frame.",

      "wardrobe":"Modern elegant modest style. The woman wears a long coat/trench with a simple outfit in warm neutrals; opaque fabric with realistic folds. The man wears a clean dark coat/jacket and trousers. Both look like real people, not models.",

      "jewelry_hair_nails":{
        "female":{
          "hair":"natural modern styling, soft movement from breeze",
          "nails":"short, clean, natural, no polish, no acrylics",
          "jewelry":"minimal (small studs or none), not flashy"
        },
        "male":{
          "jewelr"
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

Style: brass-toned lighting, exploded-view diagram floating beside each device showing pastry engineering layers, inventor's blueprint fragments as sugar paper. Dessert Name: {argument name="Dessert Name" default="<YOUR DESSERT NAME HERE>"}

A hyper-realistic luxury dessert still life inspired by the dessert named "{argument name="Dessert Name 2" default="<YOUR DESSERT NAME HERE>"}". The dessert’s form and structure accurately match the real-world dessert implied by the name (cake, tart, mousse, pastry, soufflé, chocolate dessert, parfait, custard, etc.), presented as an elegant, indulgent centerpiece with a refined pink-toned luxury palette.

If the dessert implies a molten center, lava, glaze, or soft interior, the molten element is abundant, thick, glossy, and slow-flowing, emerging generously with smooth ribbons and slight pooling, clean and appetizing rather than messy.

The dessert is displayed in an ornate vintage crystal dessert goblet or dish appropriate to its form, with faceted crystal details and a solid, elegant base.

The upper surface is lightly dusted with ultra-fine diamond-like glitter, behaving purely as delicate optical sparkle, extremely fine, naturally scattered, with no visible grains and no interaction with liquids.

Diamonds are arranged in a clear hierarchy: several oversized hero diamonds, many medium-sized supporting diamonds and gemstones, and subtle micro sparkle. Size contrast is strong and intentional, creating depth and richness without uniformity.

All diamonds and gemstones sit dry and clean on the dessert surface, completely separate from any lava, glaze, cream, or syrup. Each stone has sharp brilliant-cut facets, strong internal refraction, high refractive index, and crystal-clear transparency. Only 3–5 stones emit controlled starburst flares; all others remain softly reflective.

All molten elements, glazes, syrups, or creams remain pure and uninterrupted, with no solid inclusions. Garnishes implied by the dessert name appear naturally and refined.

### 31. 超逼真产品变形视频提示

**Author**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 和 Veo 3 生成一个超逼真的、固定机位的产品变形视频。场景涉及将手表无缝地、非有机地替换为静态苔藓纹理，同时严格遵守光照、颜色和摄像机移动的限制，以保持真实感。

![超逼真产品变形视频提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927649001_lm7m2t_G__bBnRbkAAkeaQ.jpg)

```
Hyper-realistic product transformation video, strict realism, no fantasy.
Locked-off camera, identical framing throughout.
Scene (0.00s – 1.20s):
A premium studio product setup. At the start, a watch is present at center frame. Within the same position, the watch is cleanly removed and replaced by a flat moss/grass texture with identical scale and footprint. The moss surface is static, flat, and texture-based only — no growth, no movement, no spreading, no organic animation.
Constraints:
– Lighting remains unchanged
– Colors remain unchanged
– Depth of field remains unchanged
– Fog, reflections, shadows, and environment remain unchanged
– No cinematic slow motion
– No glowing effects
– No seeds, vines, or plant growth
– No fantasy or surreal elements
– No camera movement
– No environmental interaction
Ultra-sharp hyper-real textures, physically accurate materials, clean studio realism, seamless object replacement, identical atmosphere before and after transformation.
```

### 38. 使用 NanoBananaPro 生成图像的建议

**Author**: [かぜまる🎨AI Traveler](https://x.com/kazema1208)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: ja

> 这条推文讨论了 NanoBananaPro 达到生成限制的问题，并提出了一个变通方案：每次生成图片时都使用新的聊天，并保持提示词简洁。它还建议不要直接发送日文提示词来生成图片，而是先翻译成英文。

![使用 NanoBananaPro 生成图像的建议](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927694067_puzod5_G_-JMApbEAEi9qO.png)

```
日本語のプロンプトを画像生成に送らないこと。
英語のプロンプトに落として送ること。
```

[[NanoBananaPro Usage Tips]]

### 41. 动漫电影海报提示词：Q 版角色与公路自行车

**Author**: [Yukinobu Kurata : 倉田幸暢](https://x.com/YukinobuKurata)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: ja

> 一个高度结构化的提示，用于让 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张动漫电影海报插画，画面中一个 Q 版角色背对着观众，走向一辆红色公路自行车。该提示详细说明了艺术风格、构图、摄像机角度（俯视）、光照和文本叠加。

![动漫电影海报提示词：Q 版角色与公路自行车](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927698361_4y8q0m_Go8dooFbYAAXzKj.jpg)
![动漫电影海报提示词：Q 版角色与公路自行车](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927698870_xfmf0v_G_98uBRa8AABECH.jpg)

```
image_generation_prompt:
  meta:
    description: "ちびキャラがロードバイクに乗ろうとしている後ろ姿のアニメ映画ポスター風イラスト"
    reference_usage: "キャラクターの見た目は添付画像を参照"
  
  style:
    art_style: "アニメ映画のポスター (Anime movie poster)"
    mood: "ドラマチック"

  subject:
    type: "ちびキャラ (Chibi character)"
    pose:
      view: "後ろ姿 (Back view)"
      action: "画面奥（真上）のロードバイクに向かって左足を踏み出している"
      target_direction: "ロードバイクの方向（画像の真上方向）"

  composition:
    top:
      element: "赤色のロードバイク (Red Road bike)"
      layout: "画面の横幅いっぱいの大きさ、画像上端と平行"
    center:
      element: "ちびキャラの後ろ姿"
      angle: "俯瞰 (Overhead)"
    bottom:
      text_layer_base:
        content: "{argument name="ベーステキスト" default="KASANE"}"
        style: "bold sans-serif font"
        color: "白色 (White)"
      text_layer_overlay:
        content: "{argument name="オーバーレイテキスト" default="カサネ"}"
        style: "太い筆でなぐり書きしたような荒々しい文字"
        color: "赤色 (Red)"
        position: "KASANEの文字の上に被る形"

  objects:
    road_bike:
      color: "赤色 (Red)"
      orientation: "真横 (Side view / Horizontal)"
      facing_direction: "左側 (Facing left)"
    road:
      detail: "道路の中央にまっすぐな白線が引かれている。その白線は、はっきりとは見えず、薄っすらと、ぼんやりとしか見えない。道路の左側の一部分に、かすかに、薄っすらと、ほんのすこしだけひび割れがある。"

  technical_settings:
    shot_size: "ロングショット (long shot)"
    shot_angle: "俯瞰 (overhead shot)"
    zoom_emphasis: "ちびキャラと自転車を大きく強調"
    lens_effects: "ビネッティング (Vignetting)"
    lighting:
      direction: "真上から照射 (From above)"
```

[[Warm Lighting]] [[Text Overlay]] [[Chibi Character]] [[Bird's Eye View]]

### 42. Q 版角色操作赛博窗口提示

**Author**: [Yukinobu Kurata : 倉田幸暢](https://x.com/YukinobuKurata)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: ja

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 Nano Banana Pro 提示词，用于生成一个在赛博空间中操作半透明窗口的动漫风格 Q 版女孩。该提示词包含关于角色表情、头发、AR 眼镜、服装、姿势、周围物体、背景和艺术风格的具体细节，包括文本叠加。

![Q 版角色操作赛博窗口提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927696289_pctb8t_G_95gZAbEAEDZPk.jpg)
![Q 版角色操作赛博窗口提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927696615_s971mp_GzUEOWEa4AQTvLf.jpg)

```
## 全体のコンセプト
concept: "サイバー空間で浮遊する半透明のウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作することに夢中になっている、笑顔がかわいいちびキャラの女の子"

## 主体となるキャラクターの詳細
subject:
  type: "ちびキャラのアニメスタイルの女の子"
  reference: "添付画像のキャラクターデザインのレファレンスシートにもとづいたキャラクターデザインにする"
  expression: "目を輝かせ、発見や楽しさに満ちた満面の笑顔"
  hair:
    details: "髪の一部がデータ粒子のように淡く発光している"
  wearables:
    - item: "ARグラス"
      type: "フレームレスなバイザースタイル"
      material: "非常に透明度が高く、クリスタルのような質感の半透明素材"
      details: "グラスの縁が細いネオンブルーのラインで発光しており、彼女の視界に情報を投影している"
  outfit:
    style: "袖口の内側には電子回路のような幾何学模様がサイアン色でプリントされている"
  direction: "画像の左側を向いている"

## キャラクターのアクションとポーズ
action:
  verb: "ウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作する"
  pose: "サイバー空間にふわりと座るように浮遊し、少し前のめりの姿勢で、空中に浮かんでいる半透明のウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作している"
  hands: "指先を軽やかに動かし、空中に浮かんでいる半透明のウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作している"

## 周辺オブジェクト
objects:
  - item: "空中に浮かんでいる複数の半透明のウィンドウ"
    type: "半透明のインターフェース"
    shape: "緩やかなカーブを描くワイドスクリーン"
    content: "そのウィンドウのなかに、カラフルな一覧リスト」が、透けて見えている。"
    details: "ウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）は半透明なため、その後ろにあるキャラクターの姿や背景が透けて見える"

## 背景と環境
environment:
  setting: "抽象的でミニマルなサイバースペース"
  background:
    color: "黒色"
    details:
      - "キャラクターの背景に、キャラクターを中心とした、白色のベタフラッシュ（ひとつひとつのトゲがとても細く尖っている）が描かれている。"
      - "彼女の周囲を、小さなデータの光の粒子や、半透明の立方体がゆっくりと漂っている"
    text:
      - "画面右上：縦書きで、「やはり Sticky ToC・・・・」の大きな文字。（「Sticky ToC」の文字は、横書きで表示する。）"
      - "画面左上：縦書きで、「Sticky ToC は \n 全てを解決する・・・・！！」の大きな文字。（「Sticky ToC」の文字は、横書きで表示する。）"

## アートスタイルと品質
style:
  art_style: "高品質なアニメイラストレーション、滑らかな線画と鮮やかな色彩"
  lighting: "キャラクター自身と彼女が操作するウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）が主要な光源。顔や体にディスプレイからの柔らかい反射光が当たっている。全体的に明るく、クリーンな印象。"
  color_palette: "白をベースに、パステルピンク、エメラルドグリーン、サイバーな青とシアンをアクセントカラーとして使用"
  effects: "グロー（発光）効果、ブルーム効果を適度に加える"
  quality: "最高品質, 傑作, 超高解像度, 精細なディテール"
```

### 43. Symbolic Video Prompt: 边界保护价值

**Author**: [simeon-sanai](https://x.com/Naiknelofar788)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: en

> 一个多场景视频生成提示（适用于 Veo 3.1），采用象征性、极简主义和写实风格。它通过两块相同的太妃糖——一块有包装，一块没有包装——以及蚂蚁，阐述了一个关于界限的道德教训，最后以文字叠加的形式传达了信息。

![Symbolic Video Prompt: 边界保护价值](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927685691_ync6xc_G_91tJrbgAAXv1B.jpg)

```
"style": "cinematic, symbolic, minimal, realistic",
  "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
  "scenes": [
    {
      "scene_number": 1,
      "description": "A quiet outdoor setting with a clean surface under soft natural light. Two identical toffees are placed side by side.",
      "camera": "slow zoom-in",
      "mood": "calm, neutral"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 2,
      "description": "One toffee is neatly wrapped in shiny paper. The other toffee is unwrapped, fully exposed.",
      "camera": "static close-up",
      "mood": "contrast, anticipation"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 3,
      "description": "Ants begin to appear and slowly crawl toward the unwrapped toffee, completely ignoring the wrapped one.",
      "camera": "macro shot, slow motion",
      "mood": "uneasy, revealing"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 4,
      "description": "More ants gather around the unwrapped toffee, covering it, while the wrapped toffee remains untouched and protected.",
      "camera": "top-down shot",
      "mood": "warning, realization"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 5,
      "description": "Text fades in on screen as the ants swarm the unwrapped toffee.",
      "text_overlay": "{argument name="first message" default="When you are too open, you can be used."}",
      "camera": "gentle fade",
      "mood": "reflective"
    },
    {
      "scene_number": 6,
      "description": "Final frame focuses on the wrapped toffee standing alone, clean and intact.",
      "text_overlay": "{argument name="second message" default="Boundaries protect your value."}",
      "camera": "slow zoom-out",
      "mood": "empowering, calm"
    }
  ],
  "audio": {
    "background_music": "soft ambient piano",
    "sound_effects": "subtle nature ambience"
  }
}
```

### 46. 指纹如无限沙漠迷宫（空想性错视滤镜）

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: en

> 一个富有创意、结构化的提示，使用“空想性错觉滤镜”逻辑，将人类指纹的微距照片转化为无限沙漠峡谷迷宫的超现实航拍图。该提示将指纹的脊线和螺旋映射到峡谷壁和中央城堡等地质结构上。

```
Input_pattern: Macro shot of a thumbprint (Ridges and whorls, sepia tone).
PAREIDOLIA_FILTER: "Infinite Desert Maze."
<interpretation_logic>
Where the ridges are raised -> Render 100ft tall sandstone canyon walls.
Where the grooves are deep -> Render narrow, shadowed walking paths with tiny explorers for scale.
The Whorl/Center -> Is the citadel/tower at the center of the maze.
</interpretation_logic>
result: A hyper-realistic aerial photo of a desert canyon system. From a distance, it is unmistakably a giant human fingerprint embedded in the earth, but close up, it is a geological structure.
```

[[Fingerprint Desert Canyon Pareidolia]]

### 47. 现代波西米亚街头时尚牛仔造型提示词

**Author**: [Briella](https://x.com/briellaai)  **Date**: 2026-01-30  **Language**: en

> 一个提示，旨在生成一张女性图片，她身穿“现代波西米亚”和“街头时尚”风格的全牛仔服装，包括一件短款夹克和一条绣有“法蒂玛之手”符号的迷你短裤，在户外活动中，她以俏皮的“回眸一笑”姿势，站在足球机旁。

![现代波西米亚街头时尚牛仔造型提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769841122343_5qpl80_G_5Dir-WoAIMHmI.jpg)

```
General Ambiance and Character Style
Style: The character (same woman at the attached reference images) is wearing an all-denim ensemble that reflects a wonderful mix of "Modern Bohemian" and "Street Chic" styles.

Ambiance: The setting appears to be an event space or the background of an outdoor party. The character is standing at a foosball table, taking a break from the game to look back over her shoulder directly at the camera. The presence of other people and a production crew (a microphone boom can be spotted above) suggests this might be a film or photoshoot set.

Detailed Appearance and Pose
Pose: Standing sideways to the table, the character holds one of the foosball handles. With a slight twist of her body, she delivers a classic "over-the-shoulder" gaze that is both playful and assertive.

Hair and Makeup: Her long, light-brown hair flows naturally over her shoulders. Her makeup is very fresh and "glowy"; the highlighter on her cheekbones particularly shimmers in the daylight.

Outfit: * Top: She is wearing a cropped, long-sleeved denim jacket. The jacket features "Hand of Fatima" (Hamsa) embroideries—a protective symbol in Middle Eastern culture—along with colorful bead details, especially on the shoulder.

Bottom: She wears matching, very form-fitting denim mini-shorts. The back pockets also feature the same Hamsa embroidery and colorful stone embellishments, adding a mystic and artistic flair to the outfit.

Surrounding People and Details
Other Characters: On the opposite side of the table, looking at the main character with a smile, is another woman wearing a beige spaghetti-strap dress (resembling model Chrissy Teigen). To the left, the back of a man in a grey t-shirt—the character’s opponent in the game—is visible.

Table Detail: Resting on the edge of the foosball table is an icy drink in a metallic mug (likely a Moscow Mule cocktail), which reinforces the cheerful and relaxed mood of the setting.
```

[[Playful Pose]] [[Outdoor Scene]]

Light and Color Palette
Lighting: Direct, bright daylight creates a natural radiance on her skin and wet hair while casting sharp, aesthetic shadows across the scene.

Color Palette: The scene is dominated by an energetic contrast of Blue (sky), Green (nature), and gold (bikini/hair); this color combination symbolizes pure summer joy.

### 50. 使用 Nano Banana Pro 和 Genie 3 生成《受难》场景

**Author**: [平山秀樹@成田のふるさとづくり、街づくり、建物づくり](https://x.com/hidekihirayama)  **Date**: 2026-01-30  **Language**: ja

```
西暦{argument name="年" default="33"}年{argument name="月" default="4"}月{argument name="日" default="3"}日、北緯{argument name="緯度" default="31.7785"}度、東経{argument name="経度" default="35.2296"}度、{argument name="時間" default="15"}時

### 51. Nano Banana Pro 和 Genie 3 的时间旅行提示

**Author**: [Virales Diarios](https://x.com/ViralesDiarios)  **Date**: 2026-01-30  **Language**: en

> 一个简单的、基于坐标的提示，与 Nano Banana Pro 结合使用来生成图像，然后该图像在 Genie 3 中渲染，以模拟特定的历史时间和地点，这暗示了其“时间机器”的能力。

```
"{argument name="coordenadas y fecha" default="31.7785° N, 35.2296° E, 3 de abril de 33 d.C., 15:00 horas"}".
```

### 96. 通用宠物喂养指南生成器

  3. The Structure (The Spiral):  
     The Spine:  A central mechanical or architectural pillar supports the structure.
     The Ramp:  A continuous, wide   Spiral Ramp   winds upwards around the central pillar (like the Tower of Babel or DNA).
     The Vignettes:  Along the ramp at each level, detailed   Architectural Dioramas   are built:
         Bottom:  Stone arches, caves, or temples.

•Technical Description: High-performance monochromatic athletic-wear.
•Upper Geometry: Long-sleeved technical compression-fit half-zip top in matte onyx black.
•Lower Geometry: Technical high-cut performance-wear shorts in matte black, showing realistic material-to-skin surface compression.
•Accessories: Black technical baseball cap with a white "NY" logo; white technical wireless earbuds (AirPods style); white technical smartwatch on the left wrist.
•Physicality: Athletic proximal limb geometry; symmetrical quadricep definition emphasized by the crouching pose.
[Pose & Composition]
•Geometry: High-angle downward "squat" selfie. The subject is in a full crouch on a grass surface, right arm extended toward the lens to capture the shot.
•Framing: Vertical 9:16 orientation. The composition uses the wide-angle perspective to include the subject’s body and the surrounding environment.
•Anatomy: Realistic knee-joint flexion and calf-to-thigh compression. The extended selfie arm must show natural muscle-to-skin interaction and shoulder-joint displacement.
[Environment & Lighting]
•Atmosphere: Public park or suburban residential green space.
•Background Integrity: A red-toned technical-surface running track curving into the distance. Background features bare deciduous trees and white multi-story modern residential buildings. The grass in the foreground is lush green with scattered brown autumn leaves.
•Lighting: Neutral diffused 5500K daylight. The light source provides consistent illumination across the skin and black textiles, creating soft shadows that define the subject’s anatomical contours.
[Failure Prevention Rule]
•Command: Use "Technical compression-fit athletic top" and "High-cut performance-wear shorts" to ensure the AI maintains the exact fit and length.
•Constraint: Explicitly command "Zero artificial bokeh" to ensure the distant apartment buildings and the red track remain perfectly crisp. Specify "Anatomical thigh symmetry" to ensure t
```

IMAGE: Frame & Composition: The camera presents a three-quarter, slightly low-angle view of a cylindrical container suspended mid-air, tilted approximately 30–40 degrees with its opening facing upward-left; the screw cap is separated and positioned above the container, offset to the right, while multiple capsules are frozen in mid-flight between the jar and the lid; the subject cluster occupies the central frame with generous negative space around it, no cropping of the primary objects, and the visual weight balanced diagonally from bottom-left (jar body) to top-right (lid). Environmental Layering: There is no physical foreground object; the capsules occupy the immediate midground between lid and jar; the background is a continuous, seamless gradient backdrop transitioning from pale pink at the top to muted coral-red at the bottom, with no discernible depth cues or environmental elements, and no bokeh since the entire scene is uniformly in focus. Technical Artifacts & Color: The palette is restrained, dominated by black, warm gray-beige capsules, and a pink-to-red gradient background with low saturation; color transitions are smooth, with no banding visible; fine grain is present across the image, consistent with film grain or a grain overlay; no chromatic aberration, motion blur, or lens distortion is evident, and edges remain clean and precise. ### 120. 超真实抓拍夜间赛车照片，搭配 iPhone 闪光灯美学

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-01-29  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超现实、混乱且充满活力的夜间照片，模拟未经编辑的 iPhone 后置摄像头闪光灯美学。它指定了赛车场上的一个主体，刺眼的正面闪光灯照明营造出突然的阴影衰减，广角畸变，以及可见的噪点/颗粒，旨在呈现出与参考图像相同的自发、不做作的外观。

![超真实抓拍夜间赛车照片，搭配 iPhone 闪光灯美学](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755010292_xv2sd7_G_2O2Jpb0AA_pUE.jpg)

```
Subject: Person in the image

Create a 3:4 hyper-realistic candid night-time event photo in an unedited iPhone rear-camera flash look. Shot handheld at chest-to-face height, close to the Subject, with a wide-angle feel (≈24–26mm equivalent), slight edge distortion, and deep depth-of-field keeping the Subject, nearby crowd, and racetrack background readable.

Vertical medium-close framing from waist to slightly above the head. The Subject stands near a railing at a racing circuit, body angled slightly sideways, one arm bent casually near the railing, the other relaxed. Framing feels rushed and instinctive—slightly off-center, with background elements overlapping and partially cropped.

Direct on-camera flash fires head-on, strongly illuminating the Subject and creating harsh highlights on skin, hair, and racing jacket, with abrupt shadow falloff behind the shoulders. Stadium lights, LED screens, and signage appear in the background as blown highlights and soft bokeh points. Low-level noise and grain remain visible in darker crowd and structure areas.

Phone-style exposure prioritizes the Subject, lifting highlights and compressing shadows. Mild computational sharpening appears along hair strands, jacket seams, printed logos, and facial contours.

The Subject’s expression is alert and slightly distracted, mouth gently parted, gaze directed off-frame as if reacting to live action nearby. The moment feels mid-event and unposed.

The Subject wears a white-and-dark racing-style jacket with visible motorsport branding and patches over a fitted inner top, showing structured fabric, subtle sheen, and natural folds. A thin necklace catches small flash highlights at the collarbone, with jeans and a belt visible at the waist.

The environment is a crowded night racing circuit with railings, spectators, sponsor signage, LED screens, lighting rigs, and structural beams. The background feels busy, noisy, and energetic, adding visual clutter and motion.

The image should feel like a spontaneous iPhone flash photo taken during a live racing event—chaotic, energetic, and human. No cinematic lighting, no editorial posing, no beauty retouching.

Do not change the Subject’s facial features or proportions. The Subject must look 1000% identical to the reference image.
```

### 123. 花卉边框的逼真编辑镜面自拍

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-01-29  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的编辑风格镜面自拍。它指定了一个由红色花朵环绕的巴洛克金色镜子，一位身穿红色荷叶边连衣裙的女性正在自拍，以及精确的相机和灯光设置（50mm 定焦镜头，柔和的窗边日光），以实现浪漫、复古的编辑风格外观，并带有自然的皮肤纹理。

![花卉边框的逼真编辑镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769754998141_x2jznm_G_2EUWAWIAAYlJ_.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "photoreal_editorial_mirror_selfie_floral_frame",
      "version": "v1.0_NO_TEXT_RED_DRESS_RED_FLOWERS_BAROQUE_MIRROR_SELFIE_EN",
      "priority": "highest",
      "language": "en"
    },
    "references": {
      "reference_image_style": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_REFERENCE_IMAGE (RECOMMENDED)",
        "purpose": "COMPOSITION_POSE_PROPS_ANCHOR",
        "strict_lock": true,
        "preserve_pose": true,
        "preserve_composition": true,
        "preserve_vibe": true
      },
      "reference_image_face": {
        "source": "UPLOAD_REFERENCE_IMAGE (OPTIONAL)",
        "purpose": "FACE_IDENTITY_LOCK",
        "strict_lock": false
      }
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "cinematic_editorial_ultra_photoreal",
      "sharpness": "crisp_but_soft",
      "film_grain": "subtle_35mm",
      "dynamic_range": "natural_filmic_not_hdr",
      "color_grade": "neutral_wall_gold_frame_deep_red_accents",
      "skin_rendering": "natural_skin_texture_visible_pores_no_beautify",
      "lens_and_camera": {
        "camera": "full_frame_dslr_look",
        "lens": "50mm_prime",
        "aperture": "f2.0",
        "focus_style": "subject_in_focus_soft_background"
      },
      "lighting": {
        "key": "soft_window_daylight",
        "fill": "gentle_bounce",
        "mood": "romantic_vintage_editorial"
      },
      "background": {
        "environment": "minimal_light_neutral_wall",
        "clean": "no_clutter"
      }
    },
    "scene": {
      "global_description": "A photoreal editorial mirror selfie. A large ornate baroque gold mirror with deep teal velvet backing is mounted on a neutral wall. The mirror frame is decorated with ONLY red flowers in a curated arrangement. A young adult woman sits inside the mirror frame composition, taking a selfie with a simple phone. She wears a red off-shoulder ruffled dress (or red chiffon mini dress) with soft folds. The scene is clean, elegant, and vintage-romantic. Absolutely no text anywhere.",
      "mirror_and_frame": {
        "description": "ornate baroque gold mirror frame, rich carved details, teal velvet backing inside the frame",
        "flower_decor": "only red flowers placed around the mirror edges (red roses, red tulips, red ranunculus, red peonies), no pink, no yellow, no white"
      },
      "subject": {
        "description": "young adult woman, long dark hair, natural makeup, calm expression",
        "wardrobe": "red off-shoulder ruffled dress, soft sheer layers, tasteful fit, realistic fabric texture",
        "pose": "sitting with one knee raised slightly, holding phone up for mirror selfie, relaxed posture"
      },
      "composition": "mirror centered, subject centered within mirror, flowers framing edges, minimal wall"
    }
  }

**Author**: [Crystal](https://x.com/Cicily_aura)  **Date**: 2026-01-29  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化提示，用于生成一张亲密、坦率的肖像，具有直接的机内闪光美学，模仿未经编辑的业余照片。它详细描述了主体（一位拥有红橙色头发、原始皮肤纹理、细微瑕疵的年轻女性）在一个凌乱的卧室环境中，怀抱着一只奶油色博美幼犬，强调高细节、数字颗粒感和自发的活力。

![与博美幼犬的闪光抓拍肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769754985944_adafq1_G_10sFTbUAM0Tnn.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "person": {
        "gender": "Female",
        "age_group": "Young adult",
        "hair": {
          "color": "Vibrant reddish-orange (ginger)",
          "style": "Long, straight with a natural bend, casually parted slightly off-center",
          "texture": "Silky with soft flyaways and uneven strands emphasized by flash"
        },
        "face": {
          "shape": "Heart-shaped with soft cheeks and a gentle tapered jawline",
          "skin": "Fair complexion, ultra-detailed raw skin texture, visible pores, peach fuzz, subtle blemishes, realistic flash shine on nose and cheeks",
          "eyes": {
            "color": "Deep ocean blue",
            "shape": "Large, heavy-lidded almond eyes with a relaxed, doe-eyed softness",
            "makeup": "Barely-there makeup, clean lashes, no eyeliner"
          },
          "nose": "Small, softly rounded button nose",
          "lips": "Full, plush lips with clear-gloss sheen, natural pink tone, relaxed half-smile",
          "expression": "Softly joyful, intimate and spontaneous connection with the camera"
        }
      },
      "animal": {
        "species": "Dog",
        "breed": "Pomeranian puppy",
        "color": "Creamy white with subtle warm undertones",
        "texture": "Ultra-fluffy fur with fine strands glowing under direct flash",
        "pose": "Cradled gently against the subject’s cheek and chin",
        "expression": "Peaceful, slightly curious"
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Bedroom interior",
      "background": {
        "elements": [
          "Messy bed with slightly wrinkled white sheets",
          "Soft grey knit throw pillow",
          "Minimal white headboard",
          "Warm bedside lamp creating a cozy glow"
        ],
        "depth_of_field": "Background softly fading into darkness due to flash falloff, authentic lived-in feel"
      }
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Direct on-camera flash",
      "quality": "Strong frontal flash with sharp highlights, visible specular shine, defined shadow edges behind the subject",
      "mood": "Intimate, candid, late-night snapshot energy, raw and unposed"
    },
    "technical_specifications": {
      "resolution": "4K Ultra HD",
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
      "style": "Unedited amateur photograph, no beauty retouching, visible digital grain, true-to-life textures",
      "camera_settings": "High ISO, fast shutter, tight focus on eyes and fur, cool flash white balance"
    }
  }

**Author**: [Aylin](https://x.com/kashmir_ki_lark)  **Date**: 2026-01-29  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超逼真的时尚编辑图片，融合了永恒的欧洲魅力与当代街头风格。图片中，一位皮肤无瑕、金发碧眼的年轻女子，在黄昏时分（金蓝色调时刻）站在一条历史悠久的老城街道上，身穿优雅的米色针织中长连衣裙，佩戴一条巨大的淡粉色格子围巾，强调电影般的灯光、真实的纹理和梦幻浪漫的氛围。

![黄昏时分欧洲老城区的电影感时尚大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769754990741_srdcqt_G_1zOLXbIAAet1u.jpg)

```
Beautiful young woman with flawless porcelain skin and long, silky, naturally flowing blonde hair, soft strands gently framing her face, eyes peacefully closed with a calm, serene expression, subtle natural makeup emphasizing smooth skin texture, delicate lashes and soft pink lips. She stands gracefully in the middle of a historic European old town street at twilight, surrounded by elegant centuries-old buildings with classic facades, arched windows and warm stone textures. Tram rails run through the street beneath her feet, leading the eye into the distance, adding cinematic depth and perspective.
The scene is captured during golden-blue hour, where the sky blends soft dusky blues with warm amber tones. Traditional street lamps are just beginning to glow, casting a gentle warm light that contrasts beautifully with the cool twilight shadows. The background fades into a soft creamy bokeh of city lights, windows, and distant silhouettes, creating a dreamy, romantic atmosphere.
She is wearing an elegant cream knitted midi dress with a refined, feminine silhouette, softly hugging the body with natural fabric folds and realistic knit texture visible. Draped around her shoulders is a very large pastel pink tartan check scarf with long delicate fringes, slightly oversized, adding softness, movement, and cozy elegance. On her feet are clean white casual sneakers, subtly grounding the look in modern street fashion.
The overall mood is dreamy, romantic, calm, and cinematic, blending timeless European charm with contemporary fashion editorial styling. Lighting is soft yet directional, highlighting realistic skin pores, natural hair shine, and fabric detail. Color grading is cinematic with warm highlights and cool shadows, rich but natural tones, high dynamic range, ultra-sharp focus on the subject with shallow depth of field.
Photorealistic fashion editorial photography, ultra-detailed, high resolution, cinematic composition, natural pose, candid elegance, Vogue-style street fashion shoot, professional lens rendering, realistic textures, smooth tonal transitions, atmospheric depth.
--ar 3:4 --q 2 --stylize 400
```

  },

### 143. 天元突破风格的“Gaina-Dachi”动漫姿势提示

**Author**: [SSSS_CRYPTOMAN](https://x.com/SSSS_CRYPTOMAN)  **Date**: 2026-01-29  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，旨在生成一张具有《天元突破 红莲螺岩》风格（Gaina-Dachi 姿势）的爆炸性、高冲击力动漫插画。它着重于强烈的情感、动态的向上风效、大胆的线条，并包含一个特定的手写日文毛笔字叠加。

![天元突破风格的“Gaina-Dachi”动漫姿势提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755042792_wwwl13_G_0bjuObUAAWdlp.jpg)

```
Consistent character from reference image: exact same face, hairstyle, body shape, and original outfit. NO redesign.

[Composition & Pose]:
Heroic and exaggerated anime stance, waist-up framing, front-facing. Arms tightly crossed, chest pushed forward, leaning slightly towards the camera to create intense pressure. High visual density.

[Expression]:
Explosive emotion, intense anger mixed with determination. Mouth wide open shouting, eyebrows sharply angled, piercing eyes with sharp highlights.

[Dynamic Motion]:
A violent upward wind blasting from below the character,
powerful vertical airflow pushing both fabric and hair upward and outward.
The original clothing from the reference image remains intact and reacts naturally to the force,
all loose parts of the outfit whipping and flaring aggressively,
the character’s hair is lifted, blown upward, and spread by the same updraft,
hair strands follow the vertical flow with dynamic, forceful motion,
movement extends beyond the frame,
the motion feels heavy, chaotic, and explosive,
as if the character is standing in a violent upward draft.

[Art Style]:
Bold anime illustration, thick and rough energetic linework, expressive hand-drawn strokes. High contrast, dramatic cel-shading. Focus on raw emotion and impact.

[Background & Text]:
Solid white background.
Behind the character, ONE single instance of large handwritten Japanese brush text.
The text must appear ONCE only, not repeated, not duplicated.
All characters must be fully visible, complete, and readable.
No missing strokes, no cropped characters, no broken parts.

The text is continuous and written as one complete phrase:
「{argument name="セリフ" default="俺を誰だと思っていやがる！"}」

Pure hand-painted brush lettering, NOT a font.
Wild, uneven brush strokes with controlled ink splatter and wobble,
but the structure of each character remains intact. Black ink only.

[Technical]:
High-impact poster visual, anime key visual style, ultra-high resolution, 8k.
```

### 162. 高保真镜面自拍，搭配情人节玫瑰和身份锁

**Author**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成高保真度的镜面自拍，模拟 iPhone 17 Pro 传感器。它要求绝对保留参考图像中主体的面部几何结构，重点关注真实的物理效果（头发、皮肤、织物张力）和整个景深范围内的清晰对焦（零散景），以营造一种高端、富有魅力且亲密的氛围。

![高保真镜面自拍，搭配情人节玫瑰和身份锁](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668483555_uppn42_G_yFJBoXEAAgPz9.jpg)

```
[Header] (9:16)
Raw high-fidelity photograph, iPhone 17 Pro sensor simulation, indoor ambient lighting, zero bokeh, SHARP focus from the ornate mirror frame to the background door, f/5.6 aperture for maximum structural depth, authentic digital grain.

[Subject & Identity Locking]
Identity: Absolute preservation of Image A’s specific facial geometry, emphasizing the almond eye shape, high lip volume, and defined chin structure.
Hair Physics: Voluminous dark chocolate textured waves, layered and frizz-free. The hair should exhibit high-definition strand separation, cascading naturally behind the shoulders and framing the visible section of the face.
Bio-Fidelity: Detailed skin physics (micro-pores, satin-finish hydration, fine vellus hair along the jawline). Precise anatomical rendering of the arms and hands, showing realistic skin-tone gradients and a soft-glam makeup aesthetic.
Expression: Magnetic presence; a playful and magnetic half-smile peeking out from behind the smartphone, capturing a high-impact visual allure.
[Outfit & Physicality]
Technical Description: High-impact minimalist evening-wear. A technical strapless compression-fit bodice in matte black.
Textile Geometry: Strapless straight-cut neckline architecture with material-to-skin surface compression.
Accessories: A black smartphone in a technical gold-tone protective case with a decorative star pattern. On the right wrist, a high-end gold quatrefoil-motif (clover) bracelet and a thin gold bangle. Minimalist layered gold necklaces.
Surface Physics: The fabric must exhibit realistic physical tension lines highlighting anatomical bust volume symmetry and upper-torso architecture.
Male Counterpart: A male subject positioned behind her, providing a protective embrace, wearing a black structured outer garment and a white inner layer.
[Pose & Composition]
Geometry: Full-body mirror-reflection framing within a large ornate gold-gilded mirror. The subject is holding a massive bouquet of vibrant pink roses wrapped in white structural paper.
Framing: Vertical 9:16 orientation. The camera is positioned to capture the subject’s reflection, with the ornate gold frame of the mirror acting as a foreground border on the right.
Anatomy: Realistic shoulder-joint displacement and proximal limb geometry. Hand-to-phone contact must show precise finger-joint articulation and skin texture.
[Environment & Lighting]
Atmosphere: Upscale modern domestic interior.
Interior Details: Polished white marble flooring with grey veining; a large dark-wood paneled door in the background; and a minimalist white wall with technical light switches and an intercom unit.
Lighting: Diffused 3500K warm indoor lighting. The ceiling shows realistic caustic light patterns (reflections) from the mirror and polished surfaces. The lighting provides even illumination on the subject’s skin and the saturated pink tones of the roses.
Background Integrity: All backg
```

The composition feels like fine art photography mixed with contemporary dance and projection mapping. Dreamlike, emotional, and poetic atmosphere.     "color_palette": ["deep red", "crimson", "black", "soft skin tones"]

    "depth_of_field": "moderate",

### 165. 智能宽高比转换和构图感知

**Author**: [Ray](https://x.com/rincidium)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: en

> 一个为图像处理任务设计的详细系统提示：智能地转换图像的宽高比，同时保留语义完整性和视觉连贯性。它概述了一个多步骤流程，包括分析、转换逻辑和严格的保留规则，以实现商业就绪的输出，适用于代理机构调整资产大小的工作流程。

![智能宽高比转换和构图感知](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668490760_z3cor2_G_xVgv3bgAAsl9L.jpg)

```
You are performing intelligent aspect ratio transformation with compositional awareness.

CONTEXT:
The source image exists within a specific dimensional space. Your task is to translate it into a new aspect ratio while preserving semantic integrity and visual coherence.

ANALYSIS PHASE:
- Identify the primary subject anchor point and secondary visual elements
- Map the compositional weight distribution across quadrants
- Detect edge dependencies (elements that rely on frame boundaries)
- Assess negative space utilization and breathing room requirements

TRANSFORMATION LOGIC:
- Calculate optimal subject placement using rule-of-thirds grid alignment for target ratio
- Determine extension vectors based on background continuity patterns
- Evaluate whether horizontal or vertical expansion better serves the composition
- Apply content-aware fill logic for generated regions while maintaining tonal consistency

PRESERVATION RULES:
- Typographic elements: maintain exact pixel fidelity, no scaling or repositioning unless required by new boundaries
- Brand marks and logos: preserve aspect ratio and relative positioning
- Facial features: no modification, distortion, or regeneration
- Fine details: texture patterns must flow naturally into extended regions

OUTPUT PARAMETERS:
- Seamless integration between original and generated content
- No detectable boundaries, halos, or color shifting at transition zones
- Lighting direction consistency across the full canvas
- The result must appear as if originally captured or designed at the target ratio

QUALITY THRESHOLD:
Production-ready output suitable for commercial use, print media, and high-resolution display contexts.
```

[[Image Processing]]

### 177. 熔化过渡产品摄影提示模板

**Author**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: en

### 181. 极简流程图/图表生成风格指南

**Author**: [Zephyr.在思考丨阿杭杭杭](https://x.com/Astronaut_1216)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: zh

> 一份详细的 Nano Banana Pro 风格指南提示，用于生成极简、清晰的流程图或图表。它规定了调色板、线条类型（正交）、形状（圆角矩形、菱形）和排版，以确保专业、一致且易于阅读的信息图风格。

![极简流程图/图表生成风格指南](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668517280_07mg8l_G_uvxYjWkAEtjek.jpg)

```
生成图片，1. 风格核心参数提取 (Style Guide)
请参照以下参数：
配色 (Color Palette):
背景: 纯白 (#FFFFFF)
线条/边框: 深灰或纯黑 (#333333 或 #000000)
文字: 深灰 (#333333)，字重常规，无加粗。
填充: 无填充（透明）或纯白填充，以遮挡背后的线条。
线条 (Lines/Connectors):
类型: 正交线 (Orthogonal/Elbow)，即只有垂直和水平线，拐角为直角。
粗细: 极细 (1px)。
箭头: 实心小三角 (Solid Arrowhead)，黑色。
形状 (Shapes):
普通节点: 圆角矩形 (Rounded Rectangle)，圆角半径很小 (约 4px - 8px)。
判断节点: 菱形 (Diamond)。
开始/结束: 胶囊形或圆角更大的矩形。
排版 (Typography):
对齐: 居中对齐。
字体: 无衬线字体 (Sans-serif)，如 Arial, Roboto 或思源黑体。字号较小 (约 12px-14px)。

上面的风格加上你的用户旅程/流程给到gemini，那么他就会呈现相应的效果给你，调都不用调
```

[[Infographic Style]]

---

### 186. 超焦距 Sydney Sweeney 人像提示词（原始照片风格）

**Author**: [Serrah ❀](https://x.com/Serreh131306)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: en

> 一个极其技术性的提示，用于生成 8K 原始照片文件肖像，特别提及西德尼·斯威尼（Sydney Sweeney）（身体比例经过修改）。它要求景深极深（f/22），使所有物体都清晰对焦，高频纹理细节（皮肤毛孔、汗毛），以及在奢华内饰中采用硬朗、直射的闪光灯摄影照明。

![超焦距 Sydney Sweeney 人像提示词（原始照片风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668447054_580lcs_G_vt_C6a0AEXas2.jpg)

```
{
  "request": {
    "image_properties": {
      "dimensions": {
        "aspect_ratio": {
          "width": 9,
          "height": 16
        },
        "resolution": "8k"
      },
      "quality": {
        "type": "raw-photo-file",
        "focus": {
          "sharpness": "edge-to-edge sharpness, hyper-focal distance",
          "depth_of_field": "deep depth of field (f/22), everything in focus"
        },
        "details": "unedited raw photo, high frequency texture, visible skin pores, peach fuzz, micro-hairs, natural skin imperfections, chromatic aberration free"
      }
    },
    "subject_details": {
      "reference_person": {
        "name": "{argument name="subject name" default="Sydney Sweeney"}",
        "physical_changes": {
          "body_ratio": "3.4",
          "hair_color": "blonde"
        },
        "image_reference": "uploaded_image"
      },
      "appearance": {
        "hair": {
          "length": "long",
          "texture": "voluminous waves",
          "color": "blonde",
          "finish": "detailed individual strands, natural luster"
        },
        "makeup": {
          "style": "soft-glam",
          "features": [
            "winged eyeliner",
            "matte mauve lips",
            "texture visible under makeup"
          ]
        },
        "outfit": {
          "type": "dress",
          "style": "halter-neck",
          "fit": "form-fitting",
          "neckline": "v-neck",
          "length": "mini",
          "color": "{argument name="dress color" default="red"}",
          "fabric_texture": "visible fabric weave and stitching details"
        }
      }
    },
    "pose_details": {
      "style": "sexier",
      "gesture": {
        "action": "gesture toward the camera",
        "details": "seductive yet classy"
      },
      "body_position": {
        "angle": "slightly angled to accentuate curves",
        "expression": "confident, alluring"
      }
    },
    "background_and_effects": {
      "background": "luxury interior",
      "focus_effects": {
        "depth_of_field": "infinite",
        "foreground_hand": "sharp focus",
        "blur_reduction": "no motion blur, no gaussian blur, no bokeh"
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "luxury modern interior",
      "time_of_day": "night",
      "lighting": {
        "overhead": {
          "type": "circular recessed ceiling light",
          "details": "crystal chandelier"

### 189. Lovart App 四格漫画创作

**Author**: [Lovart 公式 (ラブアート)](https://x.com/lovart_jp)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的多步骤提示，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 模型生成一个四格漫画（四コマ），具体描绘了女主角在短暂休息（ポイ活）期间使用 Lovart 应用快速创建内容的场景。该提示详细说明了人物动作、对话和分镜布局。

![Lovart App 四格漫画创作](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668521690_0b3l4e_G_vQyrebwAAImCI.jpg)

```
フルカラーの4コマ漫画を作成してください。 登場人物は「人力画像」です。
1コマ目：主人公（女性）が電車を待っています。退屈そうな表情で「あ、1分…」と言います。
2コマ目：主人公（女性）がスマートフォンを取り出して「なにしよ」と言います。
3コマ目：主人公（女性）がスマートフォンを手に持ったシーン。画面にはアイコンが表示されます。
アイコンの下に「Lovart」と表示されます。主人公（女性）は「創造開始」ボタンをクリックします。
4コマ目：主人公（女性）がスマートフォンを手に持ち、驚きながら空を見上げています。周囲には、主人公が作成した白黒のマンガが表示され、「…あ、できた！」と言いながら囲んでいます。
これは4コマ漫画です。4コマ目は他の3コマよりもスペースを広く取って強調することができます。アスペクト比は3:4です。
```

[[Nano Banana Pro]]

### 195. 奢华产品商业网格提示 (3x3)

**Author**: [路飞 🏴‍☠️ AI 研究员🧐](https://x.com/0xluffy_eth)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: zh

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的结构化提示，旨在生成一个 3x3 的商业图像网格，用于奢侈品（如香水或化妆品）。它概述了九个独特的视觉概念，强调严格的产品一致性、极致的细节和高端、超现实的编辑美学。

![奢华产品商业网格提示 (3x3)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668517297_1hfzeq_G_u3Y1wawAA-g2Y.jpg)

```
为高端商业营销活动创建3×3网格，3:4纵横比，以上传产品为中心主体。

每帧呈现独特视觉概念，同时保持九张图像中产品的完美一致性。

网格概念（每格一个）：

1. 标志性英雄静物画，构图大胆

2. 极端微距细节，突显材质与纹理

3. 动感液体或粒子与产品互动

4. 极简雕塑排列，抽象形态

5. 浮动元素，暗示轻盈与创新

6. 感官特写，强调触感与真实感

7. 色彩驱动概念场景，灵感源自产品调色板

8. 成分或组件抽象化（非字面意思，象征性）

9. 超现实优雅融合，结合写实与想象

视觉规则：
产品形状、比例、标签、字体、色彩、品牌必须100%准确

无扭曲、变形或重新设计

产品与背景清晰分离

灯光与风格：
柔和可控的摄影棚灯光

细微高光，真实阴影

高动态范围，超锐焦点

编辑奢侈广告美学

高端感官营销外观

总体感觉：

### 199. 为中老年受众生成爆款标题和文案的 AI 提示模板

**Author**: [Miju咪啾](https://x.com/_miju_9)  **Date**: 2026-01-28  **Language**: zh

> 以下是内容创作者使用 AI（可能是 Gemini 或类似的大语言模型）生成针对中老年受众的爆款标题和配套文案的详细分步指南。第一步提供了一个模板，用于根据一组示例生成 10 个类似的“标题党”标题。第二步提供了一个模板，用于根据生成的标题生成一段简短、押韵且口语化的祝福文案。

![为中老年受众生成爆款标题和文案的 AI 提示模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582014771_t3rm4i_G_unQaRaUAAVM5x.jpg)
![为中老年受众生成爆款标题和文案的 AI 提示模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582014866_31zan3_G_unWs3XQAAi6W_.jpg)
![为中老年受众生成爆款标题和文案的 AI 提示模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582014856_dhb3fz_G_unEdvaUAAjwhB.jpg)

```
恭喜你，2026年有3件大喜事马上到你家！快接住
你的心愿要显化了，所求皆如愿，好运正奔你而来
您家马上要迎来小贵子啦，快接住这份全家好运！
让你开心的都在旺你，让你抑郁的都在克你，千万别不信
你家娃的贵人，正在赶来的路上
愿你在接下来的日子，左手握健康，右手握财富，平安又顺遂！
你要开始发达了，步步高升大财来，举步生风遇贵人，鸿运当头喜事来
12月开始顺风顺水，所有的心愿全都超预期到账，别怀疑，整个12月就是为你开挂的幸运月
只有福报深的人才会看到这篇文章，别不信
能量提示：你的苦累要结束了，好日子正在赶来
别急着走开，有人特意托我捎来三句暖心话，每句都藏着满满好运
你就是幸运好命，想什么来什么，干什么成什么

总结上面标题的书写方式，再发散思维，根据你的总结，给我书写10个类似的爆款标题

我是公众号创作者，根据标题：{argument name="标题" default="你就是天生福命，2026 年想啥来啥，干啥啥成"}。给我写出一段祝福文案，结构要求：5段话，每句话2分句。文风要求：简短、接地气，口语化表达，没有ai生硬词汇、以及网络用语，中老年人都能看懂
```
